* \n * This is the ONLY thing that talks to the browser's Speech API.\n * All components (AgenticBar, Modals, Pages) subscribe to this.\n * \n * Rules:\n * 1. Only ONE recognition instance ever\n * 2. TTS always pauses STT (duplex policy)\n * 3. No auto-restart loops - controlled restart only\n * 4. All events logged to backend\n */\n\ntype VoiceState = 'idle' | 'listening' | 'processing' | 'speaking' | 'error' | 'paused';\ntype VoiceMode = 'interactive' | 'talkative' | 'text';\n\ninterface VoiceListener {\n    onStateChange?: (state: VoiceState) => void;\n    onTranscript?: (text: string, isFinal: boolean) => void;\n    onResponse?: (response: any) => void;\n    onError?: (error: string) => void;\n}\n\nclass VoiceManager {\n    private static instance: VoiceManager | null = null;\n    \n    private recognition: any = null;\n    private synthesis: SpeechSynthesis | null = null;\n    private state: VoiceState = 'idle';\n    private mode: VoiceMode = 'interactive';\n    private listeners: Set<VoiceListener> = new Set();\n    private isInitialized = false;\n    private shouldBeListening = false;\n    private currentUtterance: SpeechSynthesisUtterance | null = null;\n    private restartTimeout: any = null;\n    private lastTranscript = '';\n    \n    // Prevent multiple instances\n    private constructor() {}\n    \n    static getInstance(): VoiceManager {\n        if (!VoiceManager.instance) {\n            VoiceManager.instance = new VoiceManager();\n        }\n        return VoiceManager.instance;\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Initialize the voice system (call once on app mount)\n     */\n    init(): boolean {\n        if (this.isInitialized) {\n            console.log('[VoiceManager] Already initialized');\n            return true;\n        }\n        \n        const SpeechRecognition = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n        \n        if (!SpeechRecognition) {\n            console.error('[VoiceManager] Speech recognition not supported');\n            this.setState('error');\n            return false;\n        }\n        \n        this.synthesis = window.speechSynthesis;\n        this.recognition = new SpeechRecognition();\n        \n        // Configure recognition\n        this.recognition.continuous = true;\n        this.recognition.interimResults = true;\n        this.recognition.lang = 'en-US';\n        this.recognition.maxAlternatives = 1;\n        \n        // Event handlers\n        this.recognition.onstart = () => {\n            console.log('[VoiceManager] \ud83c\udfa4 Recognition STARTED');\n            this.setState('listening');\n        };\n        \n        this.recognition.onresult = (event: any) => {\n            let interim = '';\n            let final = '';\n            \n            for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {\n                const transcript = event.results[i][0].transcript;\n                if (event.results[i].isFinal) {\n                    final += transcript;\n                } else {\n                    interim += transcript;\n                }\n            }\n            \n            const text = final || interim;\n            const isFinal = !!final;\n            \n            if (text !== this.lastTranscript) {\n                this.lastTranscript = text;\n                this.notifyListeners('onTranscript', text, isFinal);\n            }\n            \n            if (isFinal && final.trim()) {\n                this.processTranscript(final.trim());\n            }\n        };\n        \n        this.recognition.onerror = (event: any) => {\n            // Ignore harmless errors\n            if (event.error === 'aborted' || event.error === 'no-speech') {\n                console.log('[VoiceManager] Harmless error:', event.error);\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            console.error('[VoiceManager] Error:', event.error);\n            \n            if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\n                this.notifyListeners('onError', 'Microphone access denied');\n                this.setState('error');\n                this.shouldBeListening = false;\n            }\n        };\n        \n        this.recognition.onend = () => {\n            console.log('[VoiceManager] Recognition ENDED, shouldBeListening:', this.shouldBeListening);\n            \n            // Clear any pending restart\n            if (this.restartTimeout) {\n                clearTimeout(this.restartTimeout);\n                this.restartTimeout = null;\n            }\n            \n            // Only restart if we should be listening AND not speaking\n            if (this.shouldBeListening && this.state !== 'speaking' && this.state !== 'paused') {\n                this.restartTimeout = setTimeout(() => {\n                    if (this.shouldBeListening && this.state !== 'speaking') {\n                        console.log('[VoiceManager] Restarting recognition...');\n                        this.startRecognition();\n                    }\n                }, 300); // Small delay to prevent rapid restart loop\n            } else {\n                this.setState('idle');\n            }\n        };\n        \n        this.isInitialized = true;\n        console.log('[VoiceManager] \u2705 Initialized');\n        return true;\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Subscribe to voice events\n     */\n    subscribe(listener: VoiceListener): () => void {\n        this.listeners.add(listener);\n        // Immediately notify of current state\n        listener.onStateChange?.(this.state);\n        \n        return () => {\n            this.listeners.delete(listener);\n        };\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Start listening\n     */\n    start(): void {\n        if (!this.isInitialized) {\n            this.init();\n        }\n        \n        console.log('[VoiceManager] START requested, current state:', this.state);\n        \n        // Stop any TTS first\n        this.stopSpeaking();\n        \n        this.shouldBeListening = true;\n        \n        if (this.state !== 'listening') {\n            this.startRecognition();\n        }\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Stop listening\n     */\n    stop(): void {\n        console.log('[VoiceManager] STOP requested');\n        \n        this.shouldBeListening = false;\n        \n        if (this.restartTimeout) {\n            clearTimeout(this.restartTimeout);\n this.setState('idle');\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Toggle listening\n     */\n    toggle(): void {\n        if (this.shouldBeListening || this.state === 'listening') {\n            this.stop();\n        } else {\n            this.start();\n        }\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Pause listening (for TTS)\n     */\n    pause(): void {\n        console.log('[VoiceManager] PAUSE');\n        \n        if (this.restartTimeout) {\n            clearTimeout(this.restartTimeout);\n            this.restartTimeout = null;\n        }\n        \n        try {\n            this.recognition?.stop();\n        } catch (e) {}\n        \n        this.setState('paused');\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Resume listening (after TTS)\n     */\n    resume(): void {\n        console.log('[VoiceManager] RESUME, shouldBeListening:', this.shouldBeListening);\n        \n        if (this.shouldBeListening) {\n            setTimeout(() => {\n                if (this.shouldBeListening && this.state !== 'speaking') {\n                    this.startRecognition();\n                }\n            }, 200);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Speak text (TTS) - automatically pauses STT\n     */\n    speak(text: string): void {\n        if (!this.synthesis) return;\n        \n        console.log('[VoiceManager] SPEAK:', text.substring(0, 50) + '...');\n        \n        // DUPLEX POLICY: Stop listening while speaking\n        this.pause();\n        \n        // Cancel any current speech\n        this.synthesis.cancel();\n        \n        const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n        utterance.rate = 0.95;\n        utterance.pitch = 1;\n        utterance.volume = 1;\n        \n        utterance.onstart = () => {\n            console.log('[VoiceManager] TTS started');\n            this.setState('speaking');\n        };\n        \n        utterance.onend = () => {\n            console.log('[VoiceManager] TTS ended');\n            this.currentUtterance = null;\n            \n            // DUPLEX POLICY: Resume listening after speaking\n            this.resume();\n        };\n        \n        utterance.onerror = (e) => {\n            console.error('[VoiceManager] TTS error:', e);\n            this.currentUtterance = null;\n            this.resume();\n        };\n        \n        this.currentUtterance = utterance;\n        this.synthesis.speak(utterance);\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Stop speaking\n     */\n    stopSpeaking(): void {\n        if (this.synthesis) {\n            this.synthesis.cancel();\n        }\n        this.currentUtterance = null;\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Set mode\n     */\n    setMode(mode: VoiceMode): void {\n        console.log('[VoiceManager] Mode:', mode);\n        this.mode = mode;\n        \n        if (mode === 'text') {\n            this.stop();\n        }\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Get current state\n     */\n    getState(): VoiceState {\n        return this.state;\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Get current mode\n     */\n    getMode(): VoiceMode {\n        return this.mode;\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Check if listening\n     */\n    isListening(): boolean {\n        return this.state === 'listening';\n    }\n    \n    /**\n     * Check if speaking\n     */\n    isSpeaking(): boolean {\n        return this.state === 'speaking';\n    }\n    \n    // \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n    // PRIVATE METHODS\n    // \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n    \n    private startRecognition(): void {\n        try {\n            this.recognition?.start();\n        } catch (e: any) {\n            // \"already started\" error is fine\n            if (!e.message?.includes('already started')) {\n                console.error('[VoiceManager] Start error:', e);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    private setState(newState: VoiceState): void {\n        if (this.state !== newState) {\n            console.log('[VoiceManager] State:', this.state, '\u2192', newState);\n            this.state = newState;\n            this.notifyListeners('onStateChange', newState);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    private notifyListeners(event: keyof VoiceListener, ...args: any[]): void {\n        this.listeners.forEach(listener => {\n            const handler = listener[event];\n            if (typeof handler === 'function') {\n                (handler as Function)(...args);\n            }\n        });\n    }\n    \n    private async processTranscript(text: string): Promise<void> {\n        console.log('[VoiceManager] Processing:', text);\n        this.setState('processing');\n        \n        try {\n            // Send to backend\n            const response = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/ledger/log', {\n                method: 'POST',\n                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n                body: JSON.stringify({\n                    user_type: 'boss',\n                    raw_transcript: text,\n                    page_route: window.location.pathname\n                })\n            });\n            \n            const data = await response.json();\n            this.notifyListeners('onResponse', data);\n            \n            // Speak response if in talkative mode\n            if (this.mode === 'talkative' && data?.tts_response?.text) {\n                this.speak(data.tts_response.text);\n            } else {\n                // Resume listening\n                if (this.shouldBeListening) {\n                    this.setState('listening');\n                } else {\n                    this.setState('idle');\n                }\n            }\n        } catch (e) {\n            console.error('[VoiceManager] Process error:', e);\n            this.setState(this.shouldBeListening ? 'listening' : 'idle');\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// Export singleton instance\nexport const voiceManager = VoiceManager.getInstance();\nexport default voiceManager;\nVMEOF\n\necho \"   \u2705 \"\"\necho \"\ud83c\udfa3 Creating useVoiceManager hook...\"\n\ncat > \"$VV/frontend/src/hooks/useVoiceManager.ts\" << 'HOOKEOF'\n/**\n * useVoiceManager Hook\n * \n * This is the ONLY voice hook components should use.\n * It subscribes to the global VoiceManager singleton.\n */\n\nimport { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';\nimport { voiceManager } from '../lib/VoiceManager';\n\ntype VoiceState = 'idle' | 'listening' | 'processing' | 'speaking' | 'error' | 'paused';\n\nexport function useVoiceManager() {\n    const [state, setState] = useState<VoiceState>('idle');\n    const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\n    const [lastResponse, setLastResponse] = useState<any>(null);\n    const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);\n    \n    useEffect(() => {\n        // Initialize on first use\n        voiceManager.init();\n        \n        // Subscribe to events\n        const unsubscribe = voiceManager.subscribe({\n            onStateChange: (newState) => {\n                setState(newState);\n            },\n            onTranscript: (text, isFinal) => {\n                setTranscript(text);\n            },\n            onResponse: (response) => {\n                setLastResponse(response);\n            },\n            onError: (err) => {\n                setError(err);\n            }\n        });\n        \n        return unsubscribe;\n    }, []);\n    \n    const start = useCallback(() => voiceManager.start(), []);\n    const stop = useCallback(() => voiceManager.stop(), []);\n    const toggle = useCallback(() => voiceManager.toggle(), []);\n    const speak = useCallback((text: string) => voiceManager.speak(text), []);\n    const stopSpeaking = useCallback(() => voiceManager.stopSpeaking(), []);\n    const setMode = useCallback((mode: 'interactive' | 'talkative' | 'text') => voiceManager.setMode(mode), []);\n    \n    return {\n        state,\n        transcript,\n        lastResponse,\n        error,\n        isListening: state === 'listening',\n        isSpeaking: state === 'speaking',\n        isProcessing: state === 'processing',\n        start,\n        stop,\n        toggle,\n        speak,\n        stopSpeaking,\n        setMode\n    };\n}\n\nexport default useVoiceManager;\nHOOKEOF\n\necho \"   \u2705 useVoiceManager.ts any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n        \\n        if (!SpeechRecognition) {\\n            console.error('[VoiceManager] Speech recognition not supported');\\n            this.setState('error');\\n            return false;\\n        }\\n        \\n        this.synthesis = window.speechSynthesis;\\n        this.recognition = new SpeechRecognition();\\n        \\n        // Configure recognition\\n        this.recognition.continuous = true;\\n        this.recognition.interimResults = true;\\n        this.recognition.lang = 'en-US';\\n        this.recognition.maxAlternatives = 1;\\n        \\n        // Event handlers\\n        this.recognition.onstart = () => {\\n            console.log('[VoiceManager] \\ud83c\\udfa4 Recognition STARTED');\\n            this.setState('listening');\\n        };\\n        \\n        this.recognition.onresult = (event: any) => {\\n            let interim = '';\\n            let final = '';\\n            \\n            for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {\\n                const transcript = event.results[i][0].transcript;\\n                if (event.results[i].isFinal) {\\n                    final += transcript;\\n                } else {\\n                    interim += transcript;\\n                }\\n            }\\n            \\n            const text = final || interim;\\n            const isFinal = !!final;\\n            \\n            if (text !== this.lastTranscript) {\\n                this.lastTranscript = text;\\n                this.notifyListeners('onTranscript', text, isFinal);\\n            }\\n            \\n            if (isFinal && final.trim()) {\\n                this.processTranscript(final.trim());\\n            }\\n        };\\n        \\n        this.recognition.onerror = (event: any) => {\\n            // Ignore harmless errors\\n            if (event.error === 'aborted' || event.error === 'no-speech') {\\n                console.log('[VoiceManager] Harmless error:', event.error);\\n                return;\\n            }\\n            \\n            console.error('[VoiceManager] Error:', event.error);\\n            \\n            if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\\n                this.notifyListeners('onError', 'Microphone access denied');\\n                this.setState('error');\\n                this.shouldBeListening = false;\\n            }\\n        };\\n        \\n        this.recognition.onend = () => {\\n            console.log('[VoiceManager] Recognition ENDED, shouldBeListening:', this.shouldBeListening);\\n            \\n            // Clear any pending restart\\n            if (this.restartTimeout) {\\n                clearTimeout(this.restartTimeout);\\n                this.restartTimeout = null;\\n            }\\n            \\n            // Only restart if we should be listening AND not speaking\\n            if (this.shouldBeListening && this.state !== 'speaking' && this.state !== 'paused') {\\n                this.restartTimeout = setTimeout(() => {\\n                    if (this.shouldBeListening && this.state !== 'speaking') {\\n                        console.log('[VoiceManager] Restarting recognition...');\\n                        this.startRecognition();\\n                    }\\n                }, 300); // Small delay to prevent rapid restart loop\\n            } else {\\n                this.setState('idle');\\n            }\\n        };\\n        \\n        this.isInitialized = true;\\n        console.log('[VoiceManager] \\u2705 Initialized');\\n        return true;\\n    }\\n    \\n    /**\\n     * Subscribe to voice events\\n     */\\n    subscribe(listener: {\\n            this.listeners.delete(listener);\\n        };\\n    }\\n    \\n    /**\\n     * Start listening\\n     */\\n    start(): void {\\n        if (!this.isInitialized) {\\n     \\n        this.shouldBeListening = true;\\n        \\n        if (this.state !== 'listening') {\\n            this.startRecognition();\\n        }\\n    }\\n    \\n    /**\\n     * Stop            clearTimeout(this.restartTimeout);\\n            this.restartTimeout = null;\\n        }\\n        \\n        try {\\n            this.recognition?.stop();\\n        } catch (e) {\\n            // Ignore\\n        }\\n        \\n        this.setState('idle');\\n    }\\n    \\n    /**\\n     * Toggle listening\\n     */\\n    toggle(): void {\\n        if (this.shouldBeListening || this.state === 'listening') {\\n            this.stop();\\n        } else {\\n            this.start();\\n        }\\n    }\\n    \\n    /**\\n     * Pause listening (for TTS)\\n     */\\n    pause(): void {\\n        console.log('[VoiceManager] PAUSE');\\n        \\n        if (this.restartTimeout) {\\n            clearTimeout(this.restartTimeout);\\n            this.restartTimeout = null;\\n        }\\n        \\n        try {\\n            this.recognition?.stop();\\n        } catch (e) {}\\n        \\n        this.setState('paused');\\n    }\\n    \\n    /**\\n     * Resume listening (after    }\\n    \\n    /**\\n     * Speak text (TTS) - automatically pauses STT\\n     */\\n    speak(text: string): void {\\n        if (!this.synthesis) return;\\n        \\n        console.log('[VoiceManager] SPEAK:', text.substring(0, 50) + '...');\\n        \\n        // DUPLEX POLICY: Stop listening while speaking\\n        this.pause();\\n        \\n        // Cancel any current speech\\n        this.synthesis.cancel();\\n        \\n        const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n        utterance.rate = 0.95;\\n        utterance.pitch = 1;\\n        utterance.volume = 1;\\n        \\n        utterance.onstart = () => {\\n            console.log('[VoiceManager] TTS started');\\n            this.setState('speaking');\\n        };\\n        \\n \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n    \\n    private startRecognition(): void {\\n        try {\\n            this.recognition?.start();\\n        } catch (e: any) {\\n            // \\\"already started\\\" error is fine\\n            if (!e.message?.includes('already started')) {\\n                console.error('[VoiceManager] Start error:', e);\\n            }\\n        }\\n    }\\n    \\n    private setState(newState: this.notifyListeners('onStateChange', newState);\\n        }\\n    }\\n    \\n    private notifyListeners(event: keyof VoiceListener, ...args: any[]): void {\\n        this.listeners.forEach(listener    private async processTranscript(text: string): Promise<void> {\\n        console.log('[VoiceManager] Processing:', text);\\n        this.setState('processing');\\n        \\n        try {\\n            // Send to backend\\n            const response = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/ledger/log', {\\n                method: 'POST',\\n                headers: { 'Content-Type': \\n            // Speak response if in talkative mode\\n            if (this.mode === 'talkative' && data?.tts_response?.text) {\\n                this.speak(data.tts_response.text);\\n            } this.setState('idle');\\n                }\\n            }\\n        } catch (e) {\\n            console.error('[VoiceManager] Process error:', e);\\n            this.setState(this.shouldBeListening ? 'listening' : 'idle');\\n        }\\n    }\\n}\\n\\n// Export singleton instance\\nexport const voiceManager = VoiceManager.getInstance();\\nexport default voiceManager;\\nVMEOF\\n\\necho \\\" \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83c\\udfa3 Creating useVoiceManager hook...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$VV/frontend/src/hooks/useVoiceManager.ts\\\" << 'HOOKEOF'\\n/**\\n * useVoiceManager Hook\\n * \\n * This is the ONLY voice hook components should use.\\n * It subscribes to the global VoiceManager singleton.\\n */\\n\\nimport { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';\\nimport { voiceManager } from '../lib/VoiceManager';\\n\\ntype VoiceState = 'idle' | 'listening' | 'processing' | 'speaking' | 'error' | 'paused';\\n\\nexport function useVoiceManager() {\\n    const [state, setState] = useState<VoiceState>('idle');\\n    const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\\n    const [lastResponse, setLastResponse] = useState<any>(null);\\n    const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);\\n    \\n    useEffect(() => {\\n        // Initialize on first use\\n        voiceManager.init();\\n        \\n        // Subscribe to events\\n        const unsubscribe = setTranscript(text);\\n            },\\n            onResponse: (response) => {\\n                setLastResponse(response);\\n            },\\n            onError: (err) => {\\n                setError(err);\\n            }\\n        });\\n        \\n        return unsubscribe;\\n    }, []);\\n    \\n    const start = useCallback(() => voiceManager.start(), []);\\n    const stop = useCallback(() => voiceManager.stop(), []);\\n    const toggle = useCallback(() => voiceManager.toggle(), []);\\n    const speak = useCallback((text: string) => voiceManager.speak(text), []);\\n    const stopSpeaking = useCallback(() => voiceManager.stopSpeaking(), []);\\n    const setMode = useCallback((mode: 'interactive' | 'talkative' | 'text') => voiceManager.setMode(mode), []);\\n    \\n isProcessing: state === 'processing',\\n        start,\\n        stop,\\n        toggle,\\n        speak,\\n        stopSpeaking,\\n        setMode\\n    };\\n}\\n\\nexport default \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83d\\udcdd Creating integration instructions...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$VV/frontend/VOICE_FIX_INSTRUCTIONS.md\\\" << 'MDEOF'\\n# \\ud83e\\udde0 VOICE FIX INSTRUCTIONS\\n\\n## THE PROBLEM\\nTwo voice systems (VoiceBrain + useVoice) were fighting for the microphone.\\nBrowser aborts when multiple recognition instances compete \\u2192 infinite loop.\\n\\n## THE SOLUTION\\nSingle VoiceManager singleton that OWNS the microphone.\\nAll components subscribe to it instead of creating their own recognition.\\n\\n## FILES CREATED\\n\\n1. `src/lib/VoiceManager.ts` - The singleton (ONE mic owner)\\n2. `src/hooks/useVoiceManager.ts` - React hook to use VoiceManager\\n3. `src/components/AgenticBar.tsx` - Unified voice control bar\\n\\n## HOW TO INTEGRATE\\n\\n### Step 1: Update MrVAssistant.tsx\\n\\nRemove these imports:\\n```typescript\\n// REMOVE:\\nimport { useVoice } from '../hooks/useVoice';\\nimport VoiceBrain from './VoiceBrain';\\n```\\n\\nAdd this automatically\\n\\nYou don't need to manage this manually.\\n\\n## TESTING\\n\\n1. targetY?: number;\n    onArrive?: () => void;\n}\n\nexport const WalkingCursor: React.FC<WalkingCursorProps> = ({\n    character = '\ud83d\udeb6',\n    targetX,\n    targetY,\n    onArrive\n}) => {\n    const [position, setPosition] = useState({ x: 100, y: 100 });\n    const [isWalking, setIsWalking] = useState(false);\n    const [direction, setDirection] = useState<'left' | 'right'>('right');\n    const targetRef = useRef({ x: 100, y: 100 });\n    const animationRef = useRef<number>();\n    \n    // Follow mouse\n    useEffect(() => {\n        const handleMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {\n targetRef.current.y - prev.y;\n                const distance = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);\n                \n                // Check if arrived\n                if (distance < 5) {\n 'right' : 'left');\n                \n                // Smooth follow\n                const speed = 0.08;\n                return {\n                    x: prev.x + dx * speed,\n                    y: prev.y + dy * speed\n                };\n            });\n            \n            animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);\n        };\n        \n        animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);\n        return () => {\n            if (animationRef.current) {\n                cancelAnimationFrame(animationRef.current);\n            }\n        };\n    }, [onArrive]);\n    \n    return (\n        <div\n            style={{\n                position: 'fixed',\n                left: position.x,\n                top: position.y,\n                fontSize: }\\n        };\\n        \\n        window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);\\n        return () => window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);\\n    }, [targetX,
